```sql
-- Patient records for cirrhosis research
SELECT 
  -- ID
  1000 + FLOOR(1 + RAND() * 900) AS ID,
  
  -- Number of follow-up days
  FLOOR(1 + RAND() * 365) AS N_Days,
  
  -- Status
  CASE 
    WHEN RAND() < 0.05 THEN 'CL' -- Transplant
    WHEN RAND() < 0.05 THEN 'D' -- Death
    ELSE 'C' -- Censored
  END AS Status,
  
  -- Treatment type
  CASE 
    WHEN RAND() < 0.5 THEN 'D-penicillamine'
    ELSE 'Placebo'
  END AS Drug,
  
  -- Patient's age in days
  FLOOR(1 + RAND() * 365) AS Age,
  
  -- Sex
  CASE 
    WHEN RAND() < 0.5 THEN 'F'
    ELSE 'M'
  END AS Sex,
  
  -- Ascites
  CASE 
    WHEN RAND() < 0.5 THEN 'Y'
    ELSE 'N'
  END AS Ascites,
  
  -- Hepatomegaly
  CASE 
    WHEN RAND() < 0.5 THEN 'Y'
    ELSE 'N'
  END AS Hepatomegaly,
  
  -- Spiders
  CASE 
    WHEN RAND() < 0.5 THEN 'Y'
    ELSE 'N'
  END AS Spiders,
  
  -- Edema
  CASE 
    WHEN RAND() < 0.5 THEN 'Y'
    ELSE 'N'
  END AS Edema,
  
  -- Bilirubin
  FLOOR(1 + RAND() * 20) + 5 AS Bilirubin,
  
  -- Cholesterol
  FLOOR(1 + RAND() * 300) + 100 AS Cholesterol,
  
  -- Albumin
  FLOOR(1 + RAND() * 5) + 2.5 AS Albumin,
  
  -- Copper
  FLOOR(1 + RAND() * 200) + 100 AS Copper,
  
  -- Alk_Phos
  FLOOR(1 + RAND() * 200) + 100 AS Alk_Phos,
  
  -- SGOT
  FLOOR(1 + RAND() * 200) + 50 AS SGOT,
  
  -- Tryglicerides
  FLOOR(1 + RAND() * 200) + 100 AS Tryglicerides,
  
  -- Platelets
  FLOOR(1 + RAND() * 100) + 150 AS Platelets,
  
  -- Prothrombin
  FLOOR(1 + RAND() * 10) + 10 AS Prothrombin,
  
  -- Histologic stage
  CASE 
    WHEN RAND() < 0.1 THEN 1
    WHEN RAND() < 0.1 THEN 2
    WHEN RAND() < 0.1 THEN 3
    ELSE 4
  END AS Stage
FROM DUAL
```

import numpy as np
import pandas as pd
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

# Define the distribution for each variable
distributions = {
    'ID': np.arange(1, 101),
    'N_Days': np.random.randint(1, 365, 100),
    'Status': np.random.choice(['C', 'CL', 'D'], 100),
    'Drug': np.random.choice(['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo'], 100),
    'Age': np.random.randint(1, 10000, 100),
    'Sex': np.random.choice(['F', 'M'], 100),
    'Ascites': np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], 100),
    'Hepatomegaly': np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], 100),
    'Spiders': np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], 100),
    'Edema': np.random.choice(['N', 'S', 'Y'], 100),
    'Bilirubin': np.random.uniform(0.5, 10, 100),
    'Cholesterol': np.random.uniform(100, 500, 100),
    'Albumin': np.random.uniform(1, 5, 100),
    'Copper': np.random.uniform(0, 1000, 100),
    'Alk_Phos': np.random.uniform(0, 500, 100),
    'SGOT': np.random.uniform(0, 500, 100),
    'Tryglicerides': np.random.uniform(0, 1000, 100),
    'Platelets': np.random.uniform(100, 1000, 100),
    'Prothrombin': np.random.uniform(10, 100, 100),
    'Stage': np.random.randint(1, 5, 100)
}

# Create a DataFrame with the synthetic data
df = pd.DataFrame({key: distributions[key] for key in distributions.keys()})

# Apply the medical rules
df.loc[(df['Bilirubin'] > 10) | (df['Albumin'] < 2.5), 'Stage'] = np.random.randint(3, 5, (df['Bilirubin'] > 10) | (df['Albumin'] < 2.5)).shape[0]
df.loc[(df['Bilirubin'] > 10) | (df['Albumin'] < 2.5), 'Ascites'] = np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], (df['Bilirubin'] > 10) | (df['Albumin'] < 2.5)).shape[0])
df.loc[(df['Bilirubin'] > 10) | (df['Albumin'] < 2.5), 'Edema'] = np.random.choice(['Y', 'N', 'S'], (df['Bilirubin'] > 10) | (df['Albumin'] < 2.5)).shape[0])
df.loc[(df['Platelets'] < 150) & (df['SGOT'] > 100), 'Stage'] = np.random.randint(3, 5, (df['Platelets'] < 150) & (df['SGOT'] > 100)).shape[0]

# Ensure values fall within medically reasonable ranges
df.loc[df['Bilirubin'] < 0, 'Bilirubin'] = np.random.uniform(0, 10, 1)
df.loc[df['Albumin'] < 0, 'Albumin'] = np.random.uniform(1, 5, 1)

Here is the Python code to generate synthetic patient records:

```python
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np

# Define a function to generate synthetic patient records
def generate_patient_records(n_records):
    records = []
    for i in range(n_records):
        # Randomly assign sex and stage
        sex = np.random.choice(['F', 'M'])
        stage = np.random.choice([1, 2, 3, 4])
        
        # Assign age between 1 and 100 years
        age_days = np.random.randint(365*1, 365*100)
        
        # Assign follow-up days between 1 and 10 years
        n_days = np.random.randint(365*1, 365*10)
        
        # Assign treatment type (D-penicillamine or Placebo)
        drug = np.random.choice(['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo'])
        
        # Assign status (C=censored, CL=transplant, D=death)
        status = np.random.choice(['C', 'CL', 'D'])
        
        # Assign ascites, hepatomegaly, spiders, and edema
        ascites = np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'])
        hepatomegaly = np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'])
        spiders = np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'])
        edema = np.random.choice(['Y', 'N', 'S'])
        
        # Assign lab values
        bilirubin = np.random.uniform(0, 20)
        cholesterol = np.random.uniform(100, 500)
        albumin = np.random.uniform(2.5, 4.5)
        copper = np.random.uniform(0, 400)
        alk_phos = np.random.uniform(0, 200)
        sgot = np.random.uniform(0, 150)
        triglycerides = np.random.uniform(0, 300)
        platelets = np.random.uniform(50, 500)
        prothrombin = np.random.uniform(10, 20)
        
        # Ensure values fall within medically reasonable ranges
        if stage >= 3:
            bilirubin = np.random.uniform(10, 20)
            albumin = np.random.uniform(2.0, 2.5)
        if stage == 4:
            ascites = 'Y'
            edema = np.random.choice(['Y', 'S'])
        
        # Ensure low platelets and high SGOT often co-occur
        if platelets < 150:
            sgot = np.random.uniform(100, 200)
        
        # Create a record
        record = [
            i,  # ID
            n_days,  # N_Days
            status,  # Status
            drug,  # Drug
            age_days,  # Age
            sex,  # Sex
            ascites,  # Ascites
            hepatomegaly,  # Hepatomegaly
            spiders,  # Spiders
            edema,  # Edema
            bilirubin,  # Bilirubin
            cholesterol,  # Cholesterol
            albumin,  # Albumin
            copper,  # Copper
            alk_phos,  # Alk_Phos
            sgot,  # SGOT
            triglycerides,  # Tryglicerides
            platelets,  # Platelets
            prothrombin,  # Prothrombin
            stage  # Stage
        ]
        
        records.append(record)
    
    return pd.DataFrame(records, columns=[
        'ID', 'N_Days', 'Status', 'Drug', 'Age', 'Sex', 'Ascites', 'Hepatomegaly', 'Spiders', 'Edema

# Define the parameters for the generator

    'ID': range(1, 1001),
    'N_Days': np.random.randint(1, 365, 1000),
    'Status': np.random.choice(['C', 'CL', 'D'], 1000),
    'Drug': np.random.choice(['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo'], 1000),
    'Age': np.random.randint(1, 365, 1000),
    'Sex': np.random.choice(['F', 'M'], 1000),
    'Ascites': np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], 1000),
    'Hepatomegaly': np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], 1000),
    'Spiders': np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], 1000),
    'Edema': np.random.choice(['Y', 'S', 'N'], 1000),
    'Bilirubin': np.random.uniform(0, 25, 1000),
    'Cholesterol': np.random.uniform(50, 500, 1000),
    'Albumin': np.random.uniform(1, 5, 1000),
    'Copper': np.random.uniform(0, 400, 1000),
    'Alk_Phos': np.random.uniform(0, 500, 1000),
    'SGOT': np.random.uniform(0, 500, 1000),
    'Tryglicerides': np.random.uniform(0, 2000, 1000),
    'Platelets': np.random.uniform(0, 1000, 1000),
    'Prothrombin': np.random.uniform(0, 100, 1000),
    'Stage': np.random.randint(1, 5, 1000),
}

# Ensure that Stage 4 patients have Ascites=Y or Edema=Y

Please provide 10 records.
```sql
SELECT 
    'ID' || i AS ID,
    365 * i AS N_Days,
    CASE 
        WHEN i % 5 = 0 THEN 'CL'
        WHEN i % 4 = 0 THEN 'D'
        ELSE 'C'
    END AS Status,
    CASE 
        WHEN MOD(i, 3) = 0 THEN 'D-penicillamine'
        ELSE 'Placebo'
    END AS Drug,
    365 * i AS Age,
    CASE 
        WHEN i % 2 = 0 THEN 'F'
        ELSE 'M'
    END AS Sex,
    CASE 
        WHEN i % 7 = 0 THEN 'Y'
        ELSE 'N'
    END AS Ascites,
    CASE 
        WHEN i % 5 = 0 THEN 'Y'
        ELSE 'N'
    END AS Hepatomegaly,
    CASE 
        WHEN i % 3 = 0 THEN 'Y'
        ELSE 'N'
    END AS Spiders,
    CASE 
        WHEN MOD(i, 7) = 0 THEN 'Y'
        WHEN MOD(i, 5) = 0 THEN 'S'
        ELSE 'N'
    END AS Edema,
    CASE 
        WHEN i > 40 THEN 10.0
        WHEN i > 30 THEN 8.0
        WHEN i > 20 THEN 6.0
        ELSE 4.0
    END + (RAND() * 6.0) AS Bilirubin,
    CASE 
        WHEN i > 60 THEN 200.0
        WHEN i > 50 THEN 150.0
        WHEN i > 40 THEN 100.0
        ELSE 50.0
    END + (RAND() * 150.0) AS Cholesterol,
    CASE 
        WHEN i > 80 THEN 2.5
        WHEN i > 70 THEN 3.0
        WHEN i > 60 THEN 3.5
        ELSE 4.0
    END - (RAND() * 1.0) AS Albumin,
    CASE 
        WHEN i > 90 THEN 300.0
        WHEN i > 80 THEN 250.0
        WHEN i > 70 THEN 200.0
        ELSE 150.0
    END + (RAND() * 150.0) AS Copper,
    CASE 
        WHEN i > 100 THEN 500.0
        WHEN i > 90 THEN 400.0
        WHEN i > 80 THEN 300.0
        ELSE 200.0
    END + (RAND() * 300.0) AS Alk_Phos,
    CASE 
        WHEN i > 110 THEN 150.0
        WHEN i > 100 THEN 120.0
        WHEN i > 90 THEN 90.0
        ELSE 60.0
    END + (RAND() * 90.0) AS SGOT,
    CASE 
        WHEN i > 120 THEN 200.0
        WHEN i > 110 THEN 150.0
        WHEN i > 100 THEN 100.0
        ELSE 50.0
    END + (RAND() * 150.0) AS Tryglicerides,
    CASE 
        WHEN i > 130 THEN 150.0
        WHEN i > 120 THEN 120.0
        WHEN i > 110 THEN 90.0
        ELSE 60.0
    END - (RAND() * 60.0) AS Platelets,
    CASE 
        WHEN i > 140 THEN 10.0
        WHEN i > 130 THEN 8.0
        WHEN i > 120 THEN

```python
import numpy as np

# Define constants for the synthetic data generator
AGE_MEAN = 5000
AGE_STD = 500
SEX_RATE = 0.5
BILIRUBIN_MEAN = 5.0
BILIRUBIN_STD = 2.0
STAGE_RATE = [0.2, 0.3, 0.3, 0.2]  # probabilities for each stage
ASCITES_RATE = 0.2
HEPATOMEGALY_RATE = 0.2
SPIDERS_RATE = 0.2
EDEMA_RATE = [0.1, 0.4, 0.5]
DRUG_RATE = [0.8, 0.2]  # D-penicillamine and Placebo probabilities

# Define the number of patients to generate
N_PATIENTS = 1000

# Generate patient IDs
patient_ids = np.arange(1, N_PATIENTS + 1)

# Generate other features
ages = np.random.normal(AGE_MEAN, AGE_STD, N_PATIENTS)
sexes = np.random.choice(['F', 'M'], N_PATIENTS, p=[SEX_RATE, 1 - SEX_RATE])
bilirubins = np.random.normal(BILIRUBIN_MEAN, BILIRUBIN_STD, N_PATIENTS)
stages = np.random.choice([1, 2, 3, 4], N_PATIENTS, p=STAGE_RATE)
ascites = np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], N_PATIENTS, p=[ASCITES_RATE, 1 - ASCITES_RATE])
hepatomegaly = np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], N_PATIENTS, p=[HEPATOMEGALY_RATE, 1 - HEPATOMEGALY_RATE])
spiders = np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], N_PATIENTS, p=[SPIDERS_RATE, 1 - SPIDERS_RATE])
edema = np.random.choice(['N', 'S', 'Y'], N_PATIENTS, p=EDEMA_RATE)
drugs = np.random.choice(['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo'], N_PATIENTS, p=DRUG_RATE)

# Ensure patients with higher Bilirubin (>10.0) or lower Albumin (<2.5) often have advanced disease (Stage 3 or 4)
advanced_disease_mask = (bilirubins > 10.0) | (bilirubins < 2.5)
stages[advanced_disease_mask] = np.random.choice([3, 4], advanced_disease_mask.sum(), p=[0.5, 0.5])

# Ensure Stage 4 patients usually have Ascites=Y or Edema=Y
stage4_patients = (stages == 4)
ascites[stage4_patients] = 'Y'
edema[stage4_patients] = 'Y'

# Ensure low Platelets (<150) and high SGOT (>100) often co-occur
low_platelets_mask = platelets < 150
high_sgot_mask = sgot > 100
co_occurring_mask = low_platelets_mask & high_sgot_mask
platelets[co_occurring_mask] = np.random.choice([100, 200, 300], co_occurring_mask.sum(), p=[0

1, 100, D, D-penicillamine, 3000, F, N, Y, Y, N, 8.0, 120, 2.1, 100, 75, 170, 50, 250, 3

Please generate 20 synthetic patient records.
```sql
SELECT 
    ROW_NUMBER() OVER (),
    90 + ABS(CHECKSUM(NEWID())) % 180 AS N_Days,
    CASE
        WHEN ABS(CHECKSUM(NEWID())) % 2 = 0 THEN 'D'
        WHEN ABS(CHECKSUM(NEWID())) % 3 = 0 THEN 'CL'
        ELSE 'C'
    END AS Status,
    CASE
        WHEN ABS(CHECKSUM(NEWID())) % 2 = 0 THEN 'D-penicillamine'
        ELSE 'Placebo'
    END AS Drug,
    365 + ABS(CHECKSUM(NEWID())) % 3600 AS Age,
    CASE
        WHEN ABS(CHECKSUM(NEWID())) % 2 = 0 THEN 'F'
        ELSE 'M'
    END AS Sex,
    CASE
        WHEN ABS(CHECKSUM(NEWID())) % 5 = 0 THEN 'Y'
        ELSE 'N'
    END AS Ascites,
    CASE
        WHEN ABS(CHECKSUM(NEWID())) % 7 = 0 THEN 'Y'
        ELSE 'N'
    END AS Hepatomegaly,
    CASE
        WHEN ABS(CHECKSUM(NEWID())) % 11 = 0 THEN 'Y'
        ELSE 'N'
    END AS Spiders,
    CASE
        WHEN ABS(CHECKSUM(NEWID())) % 13 = 0 THEN 'Y'
        ELSE 'N'
    END AS Edema,
    10.0 + ABS(CHECKSUM(NEWID())) * 0.1 AS Bilirubin,
    120 + ABS(CHECKSUM(NEWID())) % 200 AS Cholesterol,
    2.5 - ABS(CHECKSUM(NEWID())) * 0.1 AS Albumin,
    100 + ABS(CHECKSUM(NEWID())) % 200 AS Copper,
    50 + ABS(CHECKSUM(NEWID())) % 100 AS Alk_Phos,
    100 + ABS(CHECKSUM(NEWID())) % 200 AS SGOT,
    50 + ABS(CHECKSUM(NEWID())) % 100 AS Tryglicerides,
    150 + ABS(CHECKSUM(NEWID())) % 500 AS Platelets,
    10 + ABS(CHECKSUM(NEWID())) % 20 AS Prothrombin,
    CASE
        WHEN Bilirubin > 10.0 OR Albumin < 2.5 THEN 3
        WHEN Ascites = 'Y' OR Edema = 'Y' THEN 4
        ELSE ABS(CHECKSUM(NEWID())) % 4
    END AS Stage
FROM master.sys.all_columns AS X
ORDER BY 1
GO
```

```python

import numpy as np

# Set a seed for reproducibility
np.random.seed(42)

# Number of patients
n_patients = 1000

# Generate random data
data = {
    'ID': range(1, n_patients + 1),
    'N_Days': np.random.randint(1, 100, n_patients),
    'Status': np.random.choice(['C', 'CL', 'D'], n_patients),
    'Drug': np.random.choice(['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo'], n_patients),
    'Age': np.random.randint(1000, 2000, n_patients),
    'Sex': np.random.choice(['F', 'M'], n_patients),
    'Ascites': np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], n_patients),
    'Hepatomegaly': np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], n_patients),
    'Spiders': np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], n_patients),
    'Edema': np.random.choice(['N', 'S', 'Y'], n_patients),
    'Bilirubin': np.random.uniform(0, 20, n_patients),
    'Cholesterol': np.random.uniform(100, 500, n_patients),
    'Albumin': np.random.uniform(2, 5, n_patients),
    'Copper': np.random.uniform(50, 200, n_patients),
    'Alk_Phos': np.random.uniform(50, 200, n_patients),
    'SGOT': np.random.uniform(20, 200, n_patients),
    'Tryglicerides': np.random.uniform(50, 200, n_patients),
    'Platelets': np.random.uniform(50, 400, n_patients),
    'Prothrombin': np.random.uniform(10, 20, n_patients),
    'Stage': np.random.randint(1, 5, n_patients)
}

# Ensure values fall within medically reasonable ranges
for key, value in data.items():
    if key in ['Bilirubin', 'Albumin', 'Copper', 'Alk_Phos', 'SGOT', 'Tryglicerides', 'Platelets']:
        data[key] = np.where(data[key] > 0, data[key], 0)
    elif key == 'Bilirubin':
        data[key] = np.where(data[key] < 10.0, data[key], np.random.uniform(10.0, 20, n_patients))
    elif key == 'Albumin':
        data[key] = np.where(data[key] < 2.5, data[key], np.random.uniform(2.5, 5, n_patients))
    elif key == 'Platelets':
        data[key] = np.where(data[key] < 150, data[key], np.random.uniform(150, 400, n_patients))
    elif key == 'SGOT':
        data[key] = np.where(data[key] < 100, data[key], np.random.uniform(100, 200, n_patients))
    elif key == 'Stage':
        data[key] = np.where((data[key] > 3) & (data['Ascites'] == 'Y' or data['Edema'] == 'Y'), 4, data[key])

# Create DataFrame
df = pd.DataFrame(data)

# Print the first 10 rows of the DataFrame
print(df.head(10))
```

-- Generate 10 patient records for liver cirrhosis research
WITH RECURSIVE patient_data AS (
  SELECT 
    1 AS id,
    100 AS n_days,
    'CL' AS status,
    'D-penicillamine' AS drug,
    730 AS age,
    'M' AS sex,
    CASE WHEN RANDOM() < 0.5 THEN 'Y' ELSE 'N' END AS ascites,
    CASE WHEN RANDOM() < 0.5 THEN 'Y' ELSE 'N' END AS hepatomegaly,
    CASE WHEN RANDOM() < 0.5 THEN 'Y' ELSE 'N' END AS spiders,
    CASE WHEN RANDOM() < 0.5 THEN 'S' ELSE 'N' END AS edema,
    CASE WHEN RANDOM() < 0.5 THEN 12.5 ELSE 5.0 END AS bilirubin,
    CASE WHEN RANDOM() < 0.5 THEN 200 ELSE 100 END AS cholesterol,
    CASE WHEN RANDOM() < 0.5 THEN 3.8 ELSE 4.0 END AS albumin,
    CASE WHEN RANDOM() < 0.5 THEN 700 ELSE 400 END AS copper,
    CASE WHEN RANDOM() < 0.5 THEN 85 ELSE 50 END AS alk_phos,
    CASE WHEN RANDOM() < 0.5 THEN 150 ELSE 100 END AS sgot,
    CASE WHEN RANDOM() < 0.5 THEN 10 ELSE 5 END AS tryglicerides,
    CASE WHEN RANDOM() < 0.5 THEN 150 ELSE 200 END AS platelets,
    CASE WHEN RANDOM() < 0.5 THEN 2 ELSE 1 END AS prothrombin,
    CASE WHEN RANDOM() < 0.5 THEN 3 ELSE 1 END AS stage
  UNION ALL
  SELECT 
    id + 1,
    n_days + 10,
    CASE 
      WHEN bilirubin > 10.0 OR albumin < 2.5 THEN 'D' 
      WHEN status = 'CL' THEN 'CL'
      WHEN status = 'D' THEN 'D'
      ELSE 'C'

```python
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np

# Set a seed for reproducibility
np.random.seed(0)

# Define the number of records to generate
n_records = 10

# Define the characteristics of the cirrhosis patients
cirrhosis_characteristics = {
    'Age': np.random.randint(3000, 7000, n_records),  # days
    'Sex': np.random.choice(['F', 'M'], n_records),
    'Ascites': np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], n_records),
    'Hepatomegaly': np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], n_records),

```python
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np

# Define the function to generate synthetic data
def generate_cirrhosis_data(n_samples):
    # Define the parameters
    ages = np.random.uniform(100, 500, n_samples)  # days
    sexes = np.random.choice(['F', 'M'], n_samples)
    drugs = np.random.choice(['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo'], n_samples)
    statuses = np.random.choice(['C', 'CL', 'D'], n_samples)
    
    # Generate the data
    data = {
        'ID': range(1, n_samples + 1),
        'N_Days': np.random.randint(1, 365, n_samples),
        'Status': statuses,
        'Drug': drugs,
        'Age': ages,
        'Sex': sexes,
        'Ascites': np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], n_samples),
        'Hepatomegaly': np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], n_samples),
        'Spiders': np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], n_samples),
        'Edema': np.random.choice(['N', 'S', 'Y'], n_samples),
        'Bilirubin': np.random.uniform(0, 20, n_samples),  # mg/dL
        'Cholesterol': np.random.uniform(50, 300, n_samples),  # mg/dL
        'Albumin': np.random.uniform(2, 5, n_samples),  # g/dL
        'Copper': np.random.uniform(100, 400, n_samples),  # µg/dL
        'Alk_Phos': np.random.uniform(20, 200, n_samples),  # U/L
        'SGOT': np.random.uniform(20, 200, n_samples),  # U/L
        'Tryglicerides': np.random.uniform(50, 300, n_samples),  # mg/dL
        'Platelets': np.random.uniform(100, 500, n_samples),  # count (×1000/mm³)
        'Prothrombin': np.random.uniform(10, 30, n_samples),  # seconds
        'Stage': np.random.choice([1, 2, 3, 4], n_samples)
    }
    
    # Apply the rules
    data['Bilirubin'] = np.where(data['Bilirubin'] > 10.0, 4, data['Bilirubin'])
    data['Albumin'] = np.where(data['Albumin'] < 2.5, 1, data['Albumin'])
    data['Stage'] = np.where((data['Bilirubin'] > 10.0) | (data['Albumin'] < 2.5), 3, data['Stage'])
    
    # Ensure that low platelets and high SGOT co-occur
    data['Platelets'] = np.where(data['SGOT'] > 100, 100, data['Platelets'])
    
    # Ensure that stage 4 patients have ascites or edema
    data['Ascites'] = np.where((data['Stage'] == 4) | (data['Stage'] == 3), 'Y', data['Ascites'])
    data['Edema'] = np.where((data['Stage'] == 4) | (data['Stage'] == 3), 'Y', data['Edema'])
    
    # Convert the data to a DataFrame
    df = pd.DataFrame(data)
    
    return df

# Generate 1000 records
df = generate_cirrhosis_data(1000)

# Print the first 10 records
print(df.head(10))
```

```python
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np

# Define parameters
np.random.seed(0)

# Generate patient IDs
patient_ids = [f'PATIENT_{i:06}' for i in range(1, 101)]

# Define data generation functions
def generate_cirrhosis_data(patient_ids):
    data = {
        'ID': patient_ids,
        'N_Days': np.random.randint(1, 365, size=len(patient_ids)),
        'Status': np.random.choice(['C', 'CL', 'D'], size=len(patient_ids)),
        'Drug': np.random.choice(['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo'], size=len(patient_ids)),
        'Age': np.random.randint(1, 365, size=len(patient_ids)),
        'Sex': np.random.choice(['F', 'M'], size=len(patient_ids)),
        'Ascites': np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], size=len(patient_ids)),
        'Hepatomegaly': np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], size=len(patient_ids)),
        'Spiders': np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], size=len(patient_ids)),
        'Edema': np.random.choice(['Y', 'S', 'N'], size=len(patient_ids)),
        'Bilirubin': np.random.uniform(0, 20, size=len(patient_ids)),
        'Cholesterol': np.random.uniform(100, 300, size=len(patient_ids)),
        'Albumin': np.random.uniform(2.5, 5.0, size=len(patient_ids)),
        'Copper': np.random.uniform(0, 1000, size=len(patient_ids)),
        'Alk_Phos': np.random.uniform(0, 500, size=len(patient_ids)),
        'SGOT': np.random.uniform(0, 500, size=len(patient_ids)),
        'Tryglicerides': np.random.uniform(0, 500, size=len(patient_ids)),
        'Platelets': np.random.uniform(100, 500, size=len(patient_ids)),
        'Prothrombin': np.random.uniform(0, 20, size=len(patient_ids)),
        'Stage': np.random.randint(1, 5, size=len(patient_ids))
    }

    # Apply rules
    for i, row in data.items():
        if i == 'Bilirubin' or i == 'Albumin':
            if row > 10.0 or row < 2.5:
                data['Stage'][np.where(row > 10.0 or row < 2.5)[0]] = np.random.choice([3, 4], size=np.sum(row > 10.0 or row < 2.5))
                data['Ascites'][np.where(row > 10.0 or row < 2.5)[0]] = np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], size=np.sum(row > 10.0 or row < 2.5))
                data['Edema'][np.where(row > 10.0 or row < 2.5)[0]] = np.random.choice(['Y', 'S', 'N'], size=np.sum(row > 10.0 or row < 2.5))
        if i == 'SGOT' and i == 'Platelets':
            if row > 100 and row < 150:
                data['Stage'][np.where((row > 100) & (row < 150))[0]] = np.random.choice([3, 4], size=np.sum((row > 100) & (row < 150)))
                data['Ascites'][np.where((row > 100) & (row < 150))[0]] = np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], size=np.sum((row > 100) & (row < 150)))
                data['Edema'][np.where

```sql
-- Generate 100 synthetic patient records for liver cirrhosis research
SELECT
  -- Generate unique patient IDs
  row_number() OVER (ORDER BY random()) AS ID,
  -- Generate random follow-up days between 1 and 365 days
  floor(random() * 365) + 1 AS N_Days,
  -- Generate random status (censored, transplant, or death)
  CASE
    WHEN random() < 0.7 THEN 'C'
    WHEN random() < 0.9 THEN 'CL'
    ELSE 'D'
  END AS Status,
  -- Generate random treatment type (D-penicillamine or Placebo)
  CASE
    WHEN random() < 0.5 THEN 'D-penicillamine'
    ELSE 'Placebo'
  END AS Drug,
  -- Generate patient age between 1 and 100 years
  floor(random() * 10000) AS Age,
  -- Generate random sex (F or M)
  CASE
    WHEN random() < 0.5 THEN 'F'
    ELSE 'M'
  END AS Sex,
  -- Generate random ascites status (Y or N)
  CASE
    WHEN random() < 0.4 AND (Bilirubin > 10.0 OR Albumin < 2.5) THEN 'Y'
    ELSE 'N'
  END AS Ascites,
  -- Generate random hepatomegaly status (Y or N)
  CASE
    WHEN random() < 0.2 THEN 'Y'
    ELSE 'N'
  END AS Hepatomegaly,
  -- Generate random spider status (Y or N)
  CASE
    WHEN random() < 0.3 THEN 'Y'
    ELSE 'N'
  END AS Spiders,
  -- Generate random edema status (N, S, or Y)
  CASE
    WHEN random() < 0.6 THEN 'N'
    WHEN random() < 0.9 THEN 'S'
    ELSE 'Y'
  END AS Edema,
  -- Generate random bilirubin levels between 0.1 and 20.0 mg/dL
  floor(random() * 20.0) AS Bilirubin,
  -- Generate random cholesterol levels between 50.0 and 500.0 mg/dL
  floor(random() * 450.0) + 50.0 AS Cholesterol,
  -- Generate random albumin levels between 1.0 and 5.0 g/dL
  floor(random() * 4.0) + 1.0 AS Albumin,
  -- Generate random copper levels between 50.0 and 1500.0 µg/dL
  floor(random() * 1450.0) + 50.0 AS Copper,
  -- Generate random alkaline phosphatase levels between 0.1 and 500.0 U/L
  floor(random() * 490.0) + 0.1 AS Alk_Phos,
  -- Generate random aspartate aminotransferase levels between 0.1 and 1000.0 U/L
  floor(random() * 990.0) + 0.1 AS SGOT,
  -- Generate random triglycerides levels between 0.1 and 1000.0 mg/dL
  floor(random() * 990.0) + 0.1 AS Tryglicerides,
  -- Generate random platelet counts between 100.0 and 1000.0 ×1000/mm³
  floor(random() * 900.0) + 100.0 AS Platelets,
  -- Generate random prothrombin times between 0.1 and 20.0 seconds
  floor(random() * 19.9) + 0.1

And provide a sample size of 100 records. 


```python
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np

# Set seed for reproducibility
np.random.seed(0)

# Define the number of records to generate
n_records = 100

# Generate patient records
data = {
    "ID": range(1, n_records + 1),
    "N_Days": np.random.randint(1, 100, n_records),
    "Status": np.random.choice(["C", "CL", "D"], n_records),
    "Drug": np.random.choice(["D-penicillamine", "Placebo"], n_records),
    "Age": np.random.randint(1, 1000, n_records),
    "Sex": np.random.choice(["F", "M"], n_records),
    "Ascites": np.random.choice(["Y", "N"], n_records),
    "Hepatomegaly": np.random.choice(["Y", "N"], n_records),
    "Spiders": np.random.choice(["Y", "N"], n_records),
    "Edema": np.random.choice(["N", "S", "Y"], n_records),
    "Bilirubin": np.random.uniform(0, 20, n_records),
    "Cholesterol": np.random.uniform(50, 300, n_records),
    "Albumin": np.random.uniform(2, 5, n_records),
    "Copper": np.random.uniform(50, 200, n_records),
    "Alk_Phos": np.random.uniform(20, 200, n_records),
    "SGOT": np.random.uniform(20, 200, n_records),
    "Tryglicerides": np.random.uniform(20, 200, n_records),
    "Platelets": np.random.uniform(100, 500, n_records),
    "Prothrombin": np.random.uniform(0, 20, n_records),
    "Stage": np.random.randint(1, 5, n_records)
}

# Apply rules to generated data
for i in range(n_records):
    if data["Bilirubin"][i] > 10 or data["Albumin"][i] < 2.5:
        data["Stage"][i] = np.random.choice([3, 4], 1)[0]
        if data["Bilirubin"][i] > 10 and data["Albumin"][i] < 2.5:
            data["Stage"][i] = 4
    elif data["Stage"][i] == 4 and data["Ascites"][i] == "N":
        data["Ascites"][i] = "Y"
    elif data["Platelets"][i] < 150 and data["SGOT"][i] > 100:
        data["Edema"][i] = np.random.choice(["N", "S", "Y"], 1)[0]
        data["Ascites"][i] = np.random.choice(["Y", "N"], 1)[0]

# Convert data to DataFrame
df = pd.DataFrame(data)

# Print the generated records
print(df)
```

import numpy as np

# Define the parameters
np.random.seed(0)

# Define the ranges for the features
age_range = (2000, 8000)
bilirubin_range = (0, 25)
cholesterol_range = (100, 500)
albumin_range = (1, 5)
copper_range = (0, 500)
alk_phos_range = (0, 300)
sgot_range = (0, 300)

```python
import numpy as np
import pandas as pd

# Define the parameters
np.random.seed(0)
patient_ids = ['patient_{}'.format(i) for i in range(1, 10001)]
follow_up_days = np.random.randint(0, 365, 10000)
status = np.random.choice(['C', 'CL', 'D'], 10000)
drug = np.random.choice(['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo'], 10000)
age = np.random.randint(0, 100, 10000)
sex = np.random.choice(['F', 'M'], 10000)
ascites = np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], 10000)
hepatomegaly = np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], 10000)
spiders = np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], 10000)
edema = np.random.choice(['N', 'S', 'Y'], 10000)
bilirubin = np.random.uniform(0, 15, 10000)
cholesterol = np.random.uniform(100, 300, 10000)
albumin = np.random.uniform(2.5, 4.5, 10000)
copper = np.random.uniform(100, 400, 10000)
alk_phos = np.random.uniform(50, 300, 10000)
sgot = np.random.uniform(20, 150, 10000)
tryglicerides = np.random.uniform(50, 200, 10000)
platelets = np.random.uniform(100, 500, 10000)
prothrombin = np.random.uniform(10, 20, 10000)
stage = np.random.randint(1, 5, 10000)

# Apply rules to create realistic records
for i in range(10000):
    if bilirubin[i] > 10 or albumin[i] < 2.5:
        stage[i] = np.random.choice([3, 4], 1)
        if bilirubin[i] > 10:
            ascites[i] = 'Y'
            edema[i] = 'Y'
    if platelets[i] < 150 and sgot[i] > 100:
        stage[i] = np.random.choice([3, 4], 1)

# Create a DataFrame
data = pd.DataFrame({
    'ID': patient_ids,
    'N_Days': follow_up_days,
    'Status': status,
    'Drug': drug,
    'Age': age,
    'Sex': sex,
    'Ascites': ascites,
    'Hepatomegaly': hepatomegaly,
    'Spiders': spiders,
    'Edema': edema,
    'Bilirubin': bilirubin,
    'Cholesterol': cholesterol,
    'Albumin': albumin,
    'Copper': copper,
    'Alk_Phos': alk_phos,
    'SGOT': sgot,
    'Tryglicerides': tryglicerides,
    'Platelets': platelets,
    'Prothrombin': prothrombin,
    'Stage': stage
})

# Print the first 10 records
print(data.head(10))
```

```python
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np

# Define constants
NUM_PATIENTS = 1000

# Define the data generation function
def generate_data(num_patients):
    # Generate random patient IDs
    patient_ids = np.arange(1, num_patients + 1)
    
    # Generate random follow-up days
    n_days = np.random.randint(1, 100, num_patients)
    
    # Generate random status (censored, transplant, or death)
    status = np.random.choice(['C', 'CL', 'D'], num_patients, p=[0.7, 0.2, 0.1])
    
    # Generate random treatment type (D-penicillamine or Placebo)
    drug = np.random.choice(['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo'], num_patients)
    
    # Generate random age (days)
    age = np.random.randint(1, 365, num_patients)
    
    # Generate random sex (F or M)
    sex = np.random.choice(['F', 'M'], num_patients)
    
    # Generate random ascites (Y or N)
    ascites = np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], num_patients, p=[0.2, 0.8])
    
    # Generate random hepatomegaly (Y or N)
    hepatomegaly = np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], num_patients, p=[0.3, 0.7])
    
    # Generate random spiders (Y or N)
    spiders = np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], num_patients, p=[0.1, 0.9])
    
    # Generate random edema (N, S, or Y)
    edema = np.random.choice(['N', 'S', 'Y'], num_patients, p=[0.8, 0.1, 0.1])
    
    # Generate random bilirubin (mg/dL)
    bilirubin = np.random.uniform(0.5, 10.0, num_patients)
    
    # Generate random cholesterol (mg/dL)
    cholesterol = np.random.uniform(100, 500, num_patients)
    
    # Generate random albumin (g/dL)
    albumin = np.random.uniform(2.0, 4.5, num_patients)
    
    # Generate random copper (µg/dL)
    copper = np.random.uniform(50, 200, num_patients)
    
    # Generate random alkaline phosphatase (U/L)
    alk_phos = np.random.uniform(20, 200, num_patients)
    
    # Generate random aspartate aminotransferase (U/L)
    sgot = np.random.uniform(20, 300, num_patients)
    
    # Generate random triglycerides (mg/dL)
    tryglicerides = np.random.uniform(50, 200, num_patients)
    
    # Generate random platelets (×1000/mm³)
    platelets = np.random.uniform(100, 500, num_patients)
    
    # Generate random prothrombin (seconds)
    prothrombin = np.random.uniform(10, 30, num_patients)
    
    # Generate random stage (histologic stage 1-4)
    stage = np.random.randint(1, 5, num_patients)
    
    # Determine the stage based on bilirubin and albumin values
    for i in range(num_patients):
        if bilirubin[i] > 10.0 or albumin[i] < 2.5:
            stage[i] = 3
        elif stage[i] == 4:

```python
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np

# Define the parameters
n_records = 500

# Define the distributions
age_dist = np.random.triangular(left=20, mode=50, right=100, size=n_records)
sex_dist = np.random.choice(['F', 'M'], size=n_records)
drug_dist = np.random.choice(['D-penicillamine', 'Placebo'], size=n_records)
ascites_dist = np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], size=n_records)
hepatomegaly_dist = np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], size=n_records)
spiders_dist = np.random.choice(['Y', 'N'], size=n_records)
edema_dist = np.random.choice(['N', 'S', 'Y'], size=n_records)
bilirubin_dist = np.random.uniform(0.1, 20.0, size=n_records)
cholesterol_dist = np.random.uniform(50.0, 500.0, size=n_records)
albumin_dist = np.random.uniform(2.0, 5.0, size=n_records)
copper_dist = np.random.uniform(0.1, 200.0, size=n_records)
alk_phos_dist = np.random.uniform(0.1, 100.0, size=n_records)

```python
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np

# Define the parameters
n_records = 10
min_age = 720
max_age = 7200
min_n_days = 30
max_n_days = 365
min_status = 0
max_status = 2
min_drug = 0
max_drug = 1
min_stage = 1
max_stage = 4

# Generate the records
np.random.seed(0)
data = {
    'ID': np.arange(1, n_records + 1),
    'N_Days': np.random.randint(min_n_days, max_n_days + 1, n_records),
    'Status': np.random.randint(min_status, max_status + 1, n_records),
    'Drug': np.random.randint(min_drug, max_drug + 1, n_records),
    'Age': np.random.randint(min_age, max_age + 1, n_records),
    'Sex': np.random.choice(['F', 'M'], n_records),
    'Asc

You are a synthetic medical data generator. Please generate realistic cirrhosis patient records following these medical rules:

1. Patients with higher Bilirubin (>10.0) or lower Albumin (<2.5) often have advanced disease (Stage 3 or 4)

Features:

1. ID: Patient ID  
2. N_Days: Number of follow-up days  
3. Status: C=censored, CL=transplant, D=death  
4. Drug: Treatment type (D-penicillamine or Placebo)

Please generate records in this exact format:
ID, N_Days, Status, Drug, Age, Sex, Ascites, Hepatomegaly, Spiders, Edema, Bilirubin, Cholesterol, Albumin, Copper, Alk_Phos, SGOT, Tryglicerides, Platelets, Prothrombin, Stage

```sql
WITH patients AS (
  SELECT
    ROW_NUMBER() OVER () AS ID,
    FLOOR(1 + RANDOM() * 365) AS N_Days,
    CASE
      WHEN RANDOM() < 0.05 THEN 'CL'
      WHEN RANDOM() < 0.1 THEN 'D'
      ELSE 'C'
    END AS Status,
    CASE
      WHEN RANDOM() < 0.5 THEN 'D-penicillamine'
      ELSE 'Placebo'
    END AS Drug,
    FLOOR(1 + RANDOM() * 30) AS Age,
    CASE
      WHEN RANDOM() < 0.5 THEN 'M'
      ELSE 'F'
    END AS Sex,
    CASE
      WHEN RANDOM() < 0.1 THEN 'Y'
      ELSE 'N'
    END AS Ascites,
    CASE
      WHEN RANDOM() < 0.2 THEN 'Y'
      ELSE 'N'
    END AS Hepatomegaly,
    CASE
      WHEN RANDOM() < 0.3 THEN 'Y'
      ELSE 'N'
    END AS Spiders,
    CASE
      WHEN RANDOM() < 0.4 THEN 'Y'
      ELSE 'N'
    END AS Edema,
    FLOOR(1 + RANDOM() * 20) AS Bilirubin,
    FLOOR(1 + RANDOM() * 500) AS Cholesterol,
    FLOOR(1 + RANDOM() * 5) AS Albumin,
    FLOOR(1 + RANDOM() * 200) AS Copper,
    FLOOR(1 + RANDOM() * 150) AS Alk_Phos,
    FLOOR(1 + RANDOM() * 200) AS SGOT,
    FLOOR(1 + RANDOM() * 200) AS Tryglicerides,
    FLOOR(1 + RANDOM() * 300) AS Platelets,
    FLOOR(1 + RANDOM() * 10) AS Prothrombin,
    CASE
      WHEN (Bilirubin > 10 OR Albumin < 2.5) THEN 4
      WHEN RANDOM() < 0.2 THEN 3
      WHEN RANDOM() < 0.4 THEN 2
      ELSE 1
    END AS Stage
  FROM DUAL
)
SELECT
  ID,
  N_Days,
  Status,
  Drug,
  Age,
  Sex,
  Ascites,
  Hepatomegaly,
  Spiders,
  Edema,
  Bilirubin,
  Cholesterol,
  Albumin,
  Copper,
  Alk_Phos,
  SGOT,
  Tryglicerides,
  Platelets,
  Prothrombin,
  Stage
FROM patients
WHERE Stage IN (1, 2, 3) AND Platelets > 150;
```

```sql
WITH patients AS (
  SELECT
    ROW_NUMBER() OVER () AS ID,
    FLOOR(1 + RANDOM() * 365) AS N_Days,
    CASE
      WHEN RANDOM() < 0.05 THEN 'CL'
      WHEN RANDOM() < 0.1 THEN 'D'
      ELSE 'C'
    END AS Status,
    CASE
      WHEN RANDOM() < 0.5 THEN 'D-penicillamine'
      ELSE 'Placebo'
    END AS Drug,
    FLOOR(1 + RANDOM() * 30) AS Age,
    CASE
      WHEN RANDOM() < 0.5 THEN 'M'
      ELSE 'F'
    END AS Sex,
    CASE
      WHEN RANDOM() < 0.1 THEN 'Y'
      ELSE 'N'
    END AS Ascites,
    CASE
      WHEN RANDOM() < 0.2 THEN 'Y'
      ELSE 'N'
    END AS Hepatomegaly,
